NPCH helps facilitate the process of moving cellphone users numbers/profiles between network carriers. Network Carriers connect to the application to facilitate the automatic validation processes for the number transfer and port. The application effectively acts as a highly secure ‘clearing house’ between network carriers. NPCH has 1 instance in each country in which it is deployed, and currently it is deployed in 15 countries.
